## 📍 Overview

<p><h1><b>Prodigy Intern Tasks</b></h1> 

## Introduction 

Thanks for visiting the Prodigy Intern project repository! The repository contains the progress made during my Prodigy Infotech internship where I implemented a number of machine learning exercises using various Kaggle datasets. In the subsequent paragraphs, I will summarize the tasks I undertook, the methods I used, and when and where I encountered challenges. 

### Overview of Tasks 

1. **House Price Prediction** 
    - **Objective:** Predict the price of the house using the square feet of the house, the number of bedrooms and bathrooms, etc. 
    - **Methods:** Linear regression, feature selection, and data pre-processing. 

2. **Customer Segmentation** 
    - **Objective:** Create customer groups based on the purchase history of customers at a retail store. 
    - **Methods:** K-means clustering, feature engineering, and data visualization. 
3. **Image Classification of Cats and Dogs**
   - **Objective:** Classify images of cats and dogs.
   - **Techniques:** Support vector machine (SVM), image preprocessing, and feature extraction.

4. **Hand Gesture Recognition**
   - **Objective:** Identify and classify different hand gestures from image or video data.
   - **Techniques:** Deep learning, data normalization, and model training.

5. **Food Item Recognition and Calorie Estimation**
   - **Objective:** Recognize food items from images and estimate their calorie content.
   - **Techniques:** Convolutional neural networks (CNNs), image augmentation, and model evaluation.

### Key Outcomes

- **Predictive Models:** Developed robust models for predicting house prices and recognizing food items.
- **Clustering and Segmentation:** Successfully implemented clustering algorithms to segment customer data.
- **Image Classification:** Achieved high accuracy in classifying images of cats, dogs, and hand gestures.
- **Feature Engineering and Extraction:** Enhanced model performance through effective feature engineering and extraction techniques.

### Conclusion

This repository demonstrates the application of various machine learning models to address distinct real-world problems. The projects provided valuable hands-on experience in data preprocessing, model implementation, and evaluation. 

Feel free to explore the code and datasets provided for each task. Contributions and suggestions are welcome!

---

I would like to thank Prodigy Infotech for the opportunity to work on these exciting projects.

## 📦 Features

### Features

1. **Comprehensive Data Preprocessing**
   - Data cleaning, normalization, standardization, and categorical encoding.

2. **Feature Engineering**
   - Feature selection and creation to enhance model performance.

3. **Machine Learning Models**
   - Implementing linear regression, K-means clustering, SVMs, and CNNs for various predictive and classification tasks.

4. **Model Evaluation and Validation**
   - Using performance metrics (accuracy, precision, recall, F1-score, MAE, R-squared) and cross-validation techniques.

5. **Data Visualization**
   - EDA with Matplotlib and Seaborn, cluster visualization.

6. **Documentation and Reporting**
   - Comprehensive task documentation and a detailed README file.

## 🚀 Getting Started

***Requirements***

### Requirements

1. **Software and Libraries**
   - **Python:** Version 3.6 or higher.
   - **Jupyter Notebook or IDE:** For running and editing code (e.g., JupyterLab, VSCode).
   - **Libraries:** 
     - **Data Preprocessing:** Pandas, NumPy, Scikit-learn.
     - **Machine Learning:** Scikit-learn, TensorFlow/Keras (for deep learning).
     - **Data Visualization:** Matplotlib, Seaborn.
     - **Image Processing:** OpenCV (if required for image data handling).

2. **Hardware**
   - **Minimum Requirements:** 
     - 4 GB RAM (8 GB recommended).
     - 2 GHz Dual-Core Processor.
   - **Optional:** 
     - GPU (NVIDIA CUDA-compatible) for training deep learning models.

3. **Datasets**
   - **Task-Specific Datasets:** Downloadable from Kaggle:
     - [House Prices Detection](https://www.kaggle.com/c/house-prices-advanced-regression-techniques/data)
     - [Customer Segmentation](https://www.kaggle.com/datasets/vjchoudhary7/customer-segmentation-tutorial-in-python)
     - [Dogs vs. Cats](https://www.kaggle.com/c/dogs-vs-cats/data)
     - [LeapGestRecog](https://www.kaggle.com/gti-upm/leapgestrecog)
     - [Food-101](https://www.kaggle.com/dansbecker/food-101)

4. **Additional Tools**
   - **Version Control:** Git (for version control and collaboration).
   - **Package Manager:** pip or conda (for managing Python libraries).

Ensure you have these requirements set up to effectively work with the project and execute the provided code.

### ⚙️ Installation

1. Clone the Prodigy_Intern repository:

```sh
git clone https://github.com/vasanth-boyez/Prodigy_Intern.git
```

2. Change to the project directory:

```sh
cd Prodigy_Intern
```

3. Install the dependencies:

```sh
pip install -r requirements.txt
```

### 🤖 Running Prodigy_Intern

Use the following command to run Prodigy_Intern:

```sh
jupyter nbconvert --execute notebook.ipynb
```

### 🧪 Tests

To execute tests, run:

```sh
pytest notebook_test.py
```

---

## 🛠 Project Roadmap



#### **Week 1: Project Setup and Initial Tasks**

- **Day 1-2: Project Setup**
  - Set up the development environment (Python, IDE, libraries).
  - Install necessary libraries (Pandas, NumPy, Scikit-learn, Matplotlib, Seaborn, TensorFlow/Keras).
  - Download and organize datasets from Kaggle.

- **Day 3-5: Task-01 - House Price Prediction**
  - **Data Exploration and Preprocessing:**
    - Load and explore the dataset.
    - Handle missing values, encode categorical features, and normalize numerical features.
  - **Model Implementation:**
    - Implement a linear regression model.
    - Train the model and evaluate performance using metrics like MAE and R-squared.
  
- **Day 6-7: Documentation**
  - Document the process for Task-01.
  - Update README file with details about Task-01.

#### **Week 2: Middle Tasks**

- **Day 8-9: Task-02 - Customer Segmentation**
  - **Data Preprocessing:**
    - Clean and preprocess customer data.
    - Perform feature engineering and scaling.
  - **Model Implementation:**
    - Apply K-means clustering to segment customers.
    - Visualize clusters and analyze segmentation results.

- **Day 10-12: Task-03 - Image Classification of Cats and Dogs**
  - **Data Preprocessing:**
    - Resize and normalize images.
  - **Model Implementation:**
    - Implement and train an SVM model for image classification.
    - Evaluate model accuracy and performance.

- **Day 13-14: Documentation**
  - Document the process for Task-02 and Task-03.
  - Update README file with details about these tasks.

#### **Week 3: Final Tasks and Consolidation**

- **Day 15-17: Task-04 - Hand Gesture Recognition**
  - **Data Preprocessing:**
    - Prepare and preprocess hand gesture images or videos.
  - **Model Implementation:**
    - Develop and train a deep learning model (e.g., CNN) for gesture recognition.
    - Validate and optimize the model.

- **Day 18-20: Task-05 - Food Item Recognition and Calorie Estimation**
  - **Data Preprocessing:**
    - Preprocess food images and perform data augmentation if needed.
  - **Model Implementation:**
    - Implement and train a CNN model for food recognition and calorie estimation.
    - Evaluate model accuracy and performance.

- **Day 21: Final Review and Documentation**
  - Review and consolidate results from all tasks.
  - Finalize and update README file with complete project details.
  - Prepare a summary report of the entire project.

## 🤝 Contributing

Contributions are welcome! Here are several ways you can contribute:

- **[Submit Pull Requests](https://github.com/vasanth-boyez/Prodigy_Intern.git/blob/main/CONTRIBUTING.md)**: Review open PRs, and submit your own PRs.
- **[Join the Discussions](https://github.com/vasanth-boyez/Prodigy_Intern.git/discussions)**: Share your insights, provide feedback, or ask questions.
- **[Report Issues](https://github.com/vasanth-boyez/Prodigy_Intern.git/issues)**: Submit bugs found or log feature requests for Prodigy_intern.

<details closed>
    <summary>Contributing Guidelines</summary>

1. **Fork the Repository**: Start by forking the project repository to your GitHub account.
2. **Clone Locally**: Clone the forked repository to your local machine using a Git client.
   ```sh
   git clone https://github.com/vasanth-boyez/Prodigy_Intern.git
   ```
3. **Create a New Branch**: Always work on a new branch, giving it a descriptive name.
   ```sh
   git checkout -b new-feature-x
   ```
4. **Make Your Changes**: Develop and test your changes locally.
5. **Commit Your Changes**: Commit with a clear message describing your updates.
   ```sh
   git commit -m 'Implemented new feature x.'
   ```
6. **Push to GitHub**: Push the changes to your forked repository.
   ```sh
   git push origin new-feature-x
   ```
7. **Submit a Pull Request**: Create a PR against the original project repository. Clearly describe the changes and their motivations.

Once your PR is reviewed and approved, it will be merged into the main branch.

</details>
